Overview\\nGrafana's API key authentication and scope enforcement is implemented across multiple service layers, with primary components in the authentication client, API key service, and middleware.\\n\\n## Primary Authentication Implementation\\n\\n### API Key Client (pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go)\\nThe main API key authentication client implements the `authn.Client` interface and handles:\\n- **Authentication Flow**: The `Authenticate()` function validates API keys by:\\n  1. Extracting the token from the Authorization header (Bearer or Basic auth)\\n  2. Decoding the token (supporting both new format with `satokengen.Decode()` and legacy format with `apikeygen.Decode()`)\\n  3. Retrieving the API key from the service using `GetAPIKeyByHash()` or by name\\n  4. Validating the key via the `validateApiKey()` function\\n  5. Converting the API key to a service account identity\\n\\n- **Scope Enforcement**: The `validateApiKey()` function (lines 212-231) checks:\\n  - **Expiration**: Validates `key.Expires` timestamp against current time, returning `errAPIKeyExpired` if expired\\n  - **Revocation**: Checks `key.IsRevoked` flag, returning `errAPIKeyRevoked` if revoked\\n  - **Organization Match**: Verifies `orgID` matches `key.OrgID`, returning `errAPIKeyOrgMismatch` if not\\n  - **Service Account Binding**: Ensures the key belongs to a valid service account via `key.ServiceAccountId`\\n\\n- **Token Handling**: The `Hook()` function updates the `LastUsedAt` timestamp for API key usage tracking (throttled to 5-minute intervals)\\n\\n### API Key Service (pkg/services/apikey/)\\nThe API key service provides the backend functionality:\\n- **Model** (model.go): Defines the `APIKey` struct with fields for expiration (`Expires *int64`), revocation status (`IsRevoked *bool`), service account binding (`ServiceAccountId *int64`), and org context\\n- **Interface** (apikey.go): Defines the `Service` interface with methods: `GetAllAPIKeys()`, `AddAPIKey()`, `GetApiKeyByName()`, `GetAPIKeyByHash()`, `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate()`\\n- **Implementation** (apikeyimpl/apikey.go): Service wrapper that delegates to the store\\n- **Storage** (apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go): SQL store implementation that:\\n  - Creates API keys with optional expiration timestamps (calculated from `SecondsToLive` parameter)\\n  - Validates expiration values (rejects negative values with `ErrInvalidExpiration`)\\n  - Retrieves keys by hash or name from the database\\n  - Updates last used timestamps for tracking\\n\\n## GRPC Authentication\\n\\nThe GRPC server (pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go) provides an additional authentication layer that:\\n- Extracts API key tokens from gRPC metadata headers\\n- Uses the same API key service to validate tokens\\n- Checks for service account existence and admin role requirements\\n- Verifies service account is not disabled\\n- Loads permissions from access control service\\n\\n## Middleware and Context Handling\\n\\n### Authentication Middleware (pkg/middleware/auth.go)\\nProvides HTTP middleware for route-level authentication:\\n- `Auth()` function creates middleware enforcing login requirements\\n- Supports options for: requiring sign-in, requiring Grafana admin role, requiring non-anonymous users\\n- Handles token revocation errors and redirects\\n\\n### Context Handler (pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go)\\nCore middleware that:\\n- Initializes request context with authentication information\\n- Calls the authenticator to validate credentials\\n- Sets up the request context with identity information\\n\\n### Authentication Service (pkg/services/authn/authn.go)\\nDefines the authentication service interfaces:\\n- `Authenticator` interface for pluggable authentication clients\\n- `Service` interface for overall authentication orchestration\\n- Manages registered clients with priority-based authentication\\n- Supports post-auth and pre-logout hooks\\n\\n## Service Account Token Handling (pkg/services/serviceaccounts/)\\n\\nAPI keys are closely integrated with service accounts:\\n- Service account tokens use the same `apikey.APIKey` model\\n- Token expiration checking (pkg/services/serviceaccounts/api/token.go): `hasExpired()` function validates token expiration times\\n- Secret scanning service (pkg/services/serviceaccounts/secretscan/service.go): Filters out expired and revoked tokens from scanning\\n\\n## Scope and Authorization Framework\\n\\nThe system integrates with Grafana's access control system (pkg/services/accesscontrol/) for fine-grained authorization:\\n- API keys inherit the role of their service account\\n- Access control middleware validates permissions against scopes\\n- Supports role-based (org admin, editor, viewer) and RBAC (action + scope) authorization\\n\\n## Error Handling\\n\\nAPI key authentication defines specific error types in api_key.go:\\n- `errAPIKeyInvalid`: Invalid or malformed key\\n- `errAPIKeyExpired`: Key has passed its expiration time\\n- `errAPIKeyRevoked`: Key has been explicitly revoked\\n- `errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`: Key does not belong to the requested organization\\n\\n## Security Features\\n\\n1. **Token Format Support**: Supports both legacy and new secure token format (satokengen)\\n2. **Hash-Based Lookup**: Uses hashed key values for secure database storage\\n3. **Organization Isolation**: Enforces org-level isolation through OrgID checks\\n4. **Expiration Enforcement**: Unix timestamp-based expiration at authentication time\\n5. **Revocation Support**: Real-time revocation flag checking\\n6. **Service Account Binding**: Ties API keys to service accounts for permission inheritance\\n7. **Last Used Tracking**: Monitors API key usage patterns\\n8. **Admin Role Requirement**: GRPC API requires admin role for API key access\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3080,"cache_read_input_tokens":94854,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3080},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ab754bb2-2356-4dd1-9d44-87a386c0c7da","uuid":"5fec1e0d-27b1-4547-a11d-56902eb9ba90"}
